 ' Scientists have invented a technology that allows smartphones to be charged within seconds
 aise daur main jab smartphone kii bydaree teji se discharge hoti he, is tarah kii khoj logon ko raahat pahunchane vaali he
 There is also an Indian-origin researcher in the team of researchers
 shodhakartaaon ne ek nayaa electrode dizin kiya he jo smartphone kii badariyon ko chand seconds main hi charge kar degaa
 Under this design, energy will be stored in fast batteries like fast supercapacitors
 america kii dreggel uniwarsity ke shodhakartaaon ne is inelectrodes ko dizinkarne ke liye do dyemension vaale meterial mxene kaa prayog kiya he
 Importantly, electrodes are the main part of the battery
 iske jariye charging ke dauraan bydaree main energy store hoti he
 From here, the necessary power is available in the device and you can use the smartphone
 bydaree ke componants kaa behatar dizin wo hota he bydaree ko jaldi charge karke isamen zyada energy store karne main madad kar sake
 Researchers have designed a hydrogel electrode at the redox active site to store as much charge as possible
 maujuuda daur main smartphone charge karne main ghanton lagate hai
 However, mobile companies are constantly bringing fast charging technology
 ab hai and mid range smartfones main fast charging feechar die jate hai
 Under this, smartphones are charged about 40 percent in 10 minutes

 isliye aap aasaan rasta apanaate hai

 aap khud se puuchhie ki kya yah samajhadaari kii baat he? sochie, kisi khaali check par sin karnaa samajhadaari kahi jaaegi? aap koi cheez aasaani se hasil kar rahe hai, sirf isliye yah jaruri nahin ki aap best deal bhi paa jaaen
 So please do not speak politely to the dealer and research yourself
 sabhi tarah kii policy kii tulana kiijie, yah dekhie ki dirghakaalik lihaaj se aapke liye koun-si policy behatar hogi or iske baad apana vikalp chunie
 8
 apni policy ko laps hone dena samajhadaari nahin he-beemaa companiyaan aise car maalikon ko pasand nahin karatin, jinke paas motor beemaa policy nahin he
 Such people are considered irresponsible and consider it a risky investment
 aise main ve ooncha premium lagaakar apane ko surakshit rakhti hai
 If you let your car insurance policy get lapse, you may have to pay more than you thought
 nishchit rup se aap jo nai policy kharidenge vah sasti nahin milegi
 9
 insurance kii bandaling se madad milti he-kya aap kisi bade parivaar main rahete hai jiske paas aapas main saajha karne ke liye ek se zyada car hai? to sambhavat: aap kul beemaa par badi rakam kharch kar rahe honge
 It is better for you to ask your insurance company to provide a bundled (assembled) car insurance plan
 isse aapaki sabhi kaaron ke liye beemaa premium kam karne main madad milegi or aapaki acchhee bachat hogi
 This is a smart move, isn't it? 10
 ek company se duusari tak beemaa premium badalata rahata he-lokapriy lekin galat dharna ke vipareet, sabhi beemaa companiyaan alag-alag rate ofer karti hai
 Every insurance company has a customized risk management formula that makes it easier to determine how much to pay for coverage
 isliye kinhin bhi do beemaa companiyon kii keemat samaan nahin hoti
 Therefore, if you are taking an insurance policy without comparing the rates, then you may have to pay more
 ek acchhee motor beemaa policy yah sunishchit karti he ki aap itmeenaan se or aarthik chintaaon se mukt hokar gaadi chalaaen
 For example, Iffco Tokyo offers the best motor insurance policies that offer comprehensive protection
 in policys main ghayal hone, maut yaa third party kii property ko hue nuksaan se hone vaali sabhi tarah kii dendaree ko cover kiya jaataa he
 Apart from accidents, insurance policies of IFFCO Tokyo provide insurance for riots, fire, theft, explosion, natural disaster etc
 gaadi kharaab hone kii sthiti main sadak par hi sahaayta, chaabi gaayab hone par dupliket chaabi pradaan karne aadi jaise atirikt phaayde bhi die jate hai
 So, who wouldn't want a whole lot of policies like IFFCO Tokyo? So take full time, compare rates and choose well

 jhaansi nagar nigam seat se mahayor pad ke liye bhaajapa kii pratyaashee kiran verma ne jeet hajaar maton se ji hasil kii he jabaki elahabaad kii pratishthit nagar nigam seat par basapa sarkaar ke dauraan mantri rahe nandgopal nandi kii patni abhilaashaa gupta nandi ne bhaajapa ummidavaar kamala singh ko karaari shikast di
 Apart from this, SP Tom Independent candidate IS Tomar won from Bareilly seat
 muradabad nagar nigam seat se mahayor pad kii bhaajapa pratshashi veena agarwal ne apane nikatatam pratidwandvi pis party ke humanyu kadar ko kareeb 70,000 maton se karaari shikast di he
 While Veena Agarwal secured 99,237 votes, Congress candidate Humayun Kadar had to be satisfied with only about 30,000 votes
 muradabad ke alaava aligarh nagar nigam seat se mahayor pad kii bhaajapa pratyaashee shakuntla bharti vijayi hui hai
 He has defeated Independent candidate Razia Khan
 bharti ne razia khan ko lagbhag 40 hajaar se adhik maton se haraaya he
 BJP candidate for the post of Mayor of Ghaziabad Municipal Corporation, Teluram is leading
 yahaan matganana main dhaandhlee ke aarope ko lekar bhaajapa kaaryakartaaon ne virodh pradarshan kiya
 The comments isse pehle pradesh main chaar charnon main sampann hue nagar nikaay chunaav kii matanana shanivaar subah shuru ho gayi
 However, due to lack of proper supply of rain and electricity, counting work was affected in many districts of the state and the counting of work started late in those places
 gajiabad, meerut, kanpur main barish kii vajah se matganana kaa kaam deree se shuru hua jisase logon ne jamkar hangaamaa kiya
 For security, additional deployment of police forces was done at sensitive and susceptible counting centers
 in jagahon par police kii rapid ection force ko tainaat kiya gaya he
 BJP leaders have termed it an indication of the results of the Lok Sabha elections
 muradabad main mediakarmiyon se baatcheet karte hue nakvi ne kaha, chunaav ke baad ab jis tarah ke nattejey saamne aae hai usase aisa lagata he ki janata virdohi partiyon se hataash or niraash he
 He said that the results of the civic elections are indicative of the results of the Lok Sabha elections to be held in 2014
 bhaajapa ab puri tarah se loksabhaa chunaav ke liye taiyaar he
 Happy with the party's victory, BJP state president Laxmikant Vajpayee said that this is a victory of the people
 is jeet se aatmavishvaas badha he
 After this, we will now prepare for the Lok Sabha elections with double enthusiasm
 is bich, rajdhani lakhanu se bhaajapa ke saansad lalji tandon ne party kii jeet par khushi vyakt karte hue kaha ki nateezon se saaf ho chukaa he ki janata baaki dalon se tang aa chuki he
 Public confidence in BJP has increased and we hope that the party will do well in the Lok Sabha elections
 congress kaa ek bhi ummidavaar nagar nigam ke mahayor pad kii daud main jeet hasil nahin kar paaya
 Apart from the Congress, the Bahujan Samaj Party (BSP) -led candidate won in Allahabad, while in Bareilly, the sp-backed Independent candidate IS Tomar staked his victory
 rajya ke 12 nagar nigamon main se bhaajapa ne varanasi, lakhanu, agra, gorakhpur, jhaansi, kanpur, muradabad, meerut or aligarh main jeet kaa paracham laharaaya
 bjp's candidate Ramgopal Mohle from the prestigious Varanasi Municipal Corporation seat of the state defeated his nearest rival by around 62 thousand votes, while on the other hand, BJP candidate from Meerut Municipal Corporation seat Harikant Ahluwalia won by 77 thousand votes
 kanpur main bhi bhaajapa pratyaashee jagavir singh dron ne baari maton se jeet hasil kii
 BJP candidate for Lucknow Municipal Corporation seat, Dr
 dinesh sharma lagaataar duusari baar vijayi hue hai
 He has defeated his nearest rival and Congress candidate Neeraj Bora by nearly one lakh votes
 lakhanu ke alaava agra nagar nigam seat par bhi bhaajapa ke ummidavaar indrajit arya ne basapa samarthit ummidavaar kartaar singh ko 5000 maton se parajeet kiya
 The Gorakhpur Municipal Corporation seat has also won the BJP candidate
 bhaajapa kii ummidavaar satya pandey ne congress ke surhita kareem ko 80 hajaar se adhik maton se parajeet kiya
 bjp's candidate for the post of Mayor from Jhansi Municipal Corporation Kiran Verma won by a thousand votes, while Abhilasha Gupta Nandi, wife of Nandagopal Nandi, who was a minister during BSP government in Allahabad's prestigious Municipal Corporation seat, won BJP candidate Kamla Singh Defeated
 iske alaava bareli seat se sapa samarthit nirdaleey ummidavaar aies tomars ne jeet hasil kii he
 Veena Aggarwal, the BJP candidate for the post of Mayor from Moradabad Municipal Corporation seat, defeated Humayun Kadar of his nearest rival Peace Party by nearly 70,000 votes
 veena agarwal ne jahaan 99,237 mat hasil kiye vahiin congress ke pratyaashee humaayun kadar ko keval lagbhag 30 hajaar maton se hi santosh karnaa padaa
 Apart from Moradabad, BJP candidate for the post of mayor Shakuntala Bharti has won from Aligarh Municipal Corporation seat
 unhone nirdaleey pratyaashee razia khan ko haraaya he
 Bharti has defeated Razia Khan by over 40 thousand votes
 gajiabad nagar nigam ke mahayor pad ke bhaajapa pratyaashee teluram aage chal rahe hai
 BJP workers protested here over allegations of rigging in the counting of votes
 tippaniyan Earlier, the voting for the municipal elections, which was completed in four phases in the state, started on Saturday morning
 haalanki barish or bijli kii sahi aapurti na hone kii vajah se soobe ke kai jilon main matganana kaa kaam prabhavit hua or un jagahon par matganana kaa kaam deree se shuru hua
 Counting work started in Ghaziabad, Meerut, Kanpur due to rain due to which people created a ruckus
 suraksha ke lihaaj se samvedansheel or atisamvedansheel matganana kendron par police balon kii atirikt tainaati kii gayi thi
 Police rapid action forces have been deployed at these places
 party kii jeet se khush bhaajapa ke pradesh adhyaksh lakshmikant vaajapeyi ne kaha ki yah janata kii jeet he
 This victory has increased confidence
 iske baad ab ham dogune utsaah ke saath loksabhaa chunaav kii taiyaariyon main jute jaaenge
 Meanwhile, BJP MP Lalji Tandon from the capital Lucknow expressed happiness over the victory of the party, saying that the results have shown that the public is fed up with the rest of the parties
 janata kaa vishwaas bhaajapa main badhaa he or ham is baat kii aashaa karte hai ki loksabhaa chunaav main party acha pradarshan karegi
 Not a single Congress candidate could win the municipal mayoral race
 congress ke itar elahabaad main bahujan samaaj party (basapa) samarthit ummidavaar ne jeet hasil kii jabaki bareli main sapa samarthit nirdaleey ummidavaar aies tomars ne apni jeet kaa danka bajaayaa
 Among the 12 municipal corporations of the state, BJP swept to victory in Varanasi, Lucknow, Agra, Gorakhpur, Jhansi, Kanpur, Moradabad, Meerut and Aligarh
 rajya kii pratishthit varanasi nagar nigam seat se bhaajapa ke pratyaashee ramgopal mohale apane nikatatam pratidwandi ko kareeb 62 hajaar maton se parajeet kiya vahiin duusari ore meerut nagar nigam seat se bhaajapa ummidavaar harikant ahaluwalia ne 77 hajaar maton se jeet hasil kii he
 In Kanpur too, BJP candidate Jagveer Singh Drona won with heavy votes
 lakhanu nagar nigam seat par bhaajapa ke ummidavaar da
 Dinesh Sharma has emerged victorious for the second time in a row
 unhone apane nikatatam pratidwandi or congress ke ummidavaar niraj bora ko lagbhag ek lakh maton se haraaya he
 Apart from Lucknow, BJP candidate Indrajit Arya also defeated bsp-backed candidate Kartar Singh by 5000 votes in Agra Municipal Corporation seat
 gorakhpur nagar nigam seat par bhi bhaajapa ke pratyaashee ne apana paracham laharaaya he
 BJP candidate Satya Pandey defeated Surhita Karim of Congress by more than 80 thousand votes
 jhaansi nagar nigam seat se mahayor pad ke liye bhaajapa kii pratyaashee kiran verma ne jeet hajaar maton se ji hasil kii he jabaki elahabaad kii pratishthit nagar nigam seat par basapa sarkaar ke dauraan mantri rahe nandgopal nandi kii patni abhilaashaa gupta nandi ne bhaajapa ummidavaar kamala singh ko karaari shikast di
 Apart from this, SP Tom Independent candidate IS Tomar won from Bareilly seat
 muradabad nagar nigam seat se mahayor pad kii bhaajapa pratshashi veena agarwal ne apane nikatatam pratidwandvi pis party ke humanyu kadar ko kareeb 70,000 maton se karaari shikast di he
 While Veena Agarwal secured 99,237 votes, Congress candidate Humayun Kadar had to be satisfied with only about 30,000 votes
 muradabad ke alaava aligarh nagar nigam seat se mahayor pad kii bhaajapa pratyaashee shakuntla bharti vijayi hui hai
 He has defeated Independent candidate Razia Khan
 bharti ne razia khan ko lagbhag 40 hajaar se adhik maton se haraaya he
 BJP candidate for the post of Mayor of Ghaziabad Municipal Corporation, Teluram is leading
 yahaan matganana main dhaandhlee ke aarope ko lekar bhaajapa kaaryakartaaon ne virodh pradarshan kiya
 The comments isse pehle pradesh main chaar charnon main sampann hue nagar nikaay chunaav kii matanana shanivaar subah shuru ho gayi
 However, due to lack of proper supply of rain and electricity, counting work was affected in many districts of the state and the counting of work started late in those places
 gajiabad, meerut, kanpur main barish kii vajah se matganana kaa kaam deree se shuru hua jisase logon ne jamkar hangaamaa kiya

 kaam karte hue yaa kahin se nikalate hue kya makadi kaa jaala aap par chipak jaataa he
 If yes, then you must surely understand how difficult it is to remove it
 makadi apane shikaar ko fansaane ke liye jaal bunati he
 Small insects are easily trapped in this trap
 inakeedon kaa jaalase nikalnaa kaaphi mushkil hota he
 But if you have ever looked closely, you must have found that the spider itself easily roams from one place to another in that trap
 kya aapako pataa he ki aisa kyon hota he?makadi kaa puraa jaal chipakane vaale nahin hota he
 She weaves only a small part of it
 vahiin, iske alaava vaisaa hissaa jahaan makadi khud aaraam se rahati he, vah binachipachipe padaarthke banaaya jaataa he
 So she gets into it easily
 vaise apane hi jaal main funsane se bachane ke liye makadi ek or tarkeeb nikaalati he
 She cleans her feet very well daily to remove dust and other particles
 kuch vaigyanik maanate hai ki makadi kaa pair taileey hota he isliye vah jaal main nahin fansati or isamen gumti rahati he
 But the truth is that spiders do not have oil glands (glands)
 vahiin kuch vaigyanik isaki vajah makadi kii taangon par maujuud baalo ko maanate hai jin par jaale kii chipchipahat kaa koi asar nahin hota he
 The High Court has slammed the Delhi government for not making any rules for how the children of EWS category people should get admission in private schools built on government land from class 2 to 12th
 hoicourt ne sarkaar ko yah sunishchit karne kaa aadesh diya he ki kaksha 2 se 12veen tak kii kakshaon main kam aay varg (EWS) or vanchit samooh ke bacchon kaa bhi daakhila ho
 The High Court, in its interim order, has also ordered all the schools built on government land to put boards outside its schools and give details of vacant seats on the board every week
 saath hi ye byora har saptaah dilli sarkaar kii website par bhi apadet kiya jaae
 The High Court has asked all schools to upload their annual accounts on the government's website
 hoicourt ne dilli sarkaar or shiksha nideshaalay ko bhi nirdesh diya he ki is aadesh par turant amal kiya jaae
 The High Court has given this order on the petition of NGO Justice for All
 yachika main aarope he ki rajdhani ke nijee skulon main EWS ke liye kaksha 1 tak tak admician ko lekar niyamon kaa paalan hota he, lekin duusari ke baad kakshaon main daakhila kaise ho, is bare main hoicourt ke kai adeshon ke baavjood sarkaar ne abhi tak niyam nahin banaae he or didie kii jameen par bane kareeb 400 privet skool iskaa khulaa phayda uthaa rahe hai
 As a result, every year about 20 thousand children of low income group (EWS) and disadvantaged group in private schools are being killed in Delhi
 hoicourt main daayar kii gai yachika main dilli sarkaar par sarkari jameen par bane nijee skulon main EWS shrenee kii kakshaon main hone vaale daakhila par udaseenta baratane kaa aarope lagaaya gaya he
 On behalf of the organization, petitioner Khagesh Jha has demanded in the petition from the High Court to monitor the admission in EWS category itself
 unhone iske saath hi duusari va upar kii kakshaon main daakhila kaise ho, iske liye sarkaar ko niyam va kaayade banane kaa aadesh dene kii bhi maang kii he
 Khagesh Jha said that in December 2012, the High Court had requested the Delhi government to ensure admission in private schools built on government land from class II to class 12 in EWS category as well
 yachika main kaha gaya he ki sarkaar ne disambar, 2012 main adhisuchana jari kar sabhi skulon ko nirdesh diya tha ki duusari kaksha se 12veen tak kii sabhi kakshaon main hone vaale daakhila main EWS shrenee ke bhi bacchon ko daakhila diya jaae
 But the government has not yet made any rules about how to get admission
 niyam kaayade na hone se nijee skulon main har saal duusari kaksha se 12veen tak kii kakshaon main EWS shrenee kii lagbhag 20 hajaar siten khaali rah jaati hai
 The petition states that after the seats remain vacant for one year, the school management gives admission to the children of general category next year
 hoicourt ne sarkaar ko yah bhi bataane kaa aadesh diya he, duusari kaksha se 12veen tak kii kakshaon main daakhila kaise ho, is bare main abtak niyam kaayade kyon nahi banaae
 The petition said that the Central Information Commission and the High Court had ordered private schools built on the land of all ddas to upload the information of vacant seats on the website of the Delhi government every week
 lekin koi bhi skool sahi se paalan nahin kar rahaa he
 Therefore, people in the EWS category are unable to know in which schools many seats are vacant
 yachika main daawa kiya gaya he ki pichley ek saal se sarkaar ke website par siton ke bare main koi apadet nahin hua he
 The Supreme Court on Friday has now ordered further ban on IIT counseling and admission in connection with the examination under JEE (advanced)
